			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin was 2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">%, a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">n inc</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">rease from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">23.5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">crease was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the benefit of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">sales leverage</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and, to a lesser extent, lower delivery fees</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> associated with </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">a &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">lower </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">volume of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">delivery </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">transactions</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">food </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">costs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and increases in hourly wages.</font>

			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">255 to 285 new restaurant openings</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Definitions</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> following definitions apply to these terms as used throughout this release:</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Comparable restaurant sales, or sales comps, and comparable restaurant transactions, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represent the change in period-</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">over-period total revenue or transactions for restaurants in operation for at least 13 full calendar months.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Average restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">refer to the average trailing 12-month food and beverage revenue for restaurants in operation for at least 12 full calendar months.</font><a name="_Hlk74719682"></a></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represents total revenue less direct restaurant operating costs, expressed as a percent of total revenue.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Digital sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> represent food and beverage revenue generated through the Chipotle website, Chipotle app or third-party delivery aggregators. Digital sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">includes revenue deferrals associated with Chipotle Rewards. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">In-restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represent food and beverage revenue generated on-premise. In-restaurant sales includes revenue deferrals associated with Chipotle Rewards. </font></p></td></tr></table></div></div><div style="margin-left:36pt;margin-right:36pt;">

		</p>

An archived webcast will be available approximately one hour after the end of the call.</font>

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">nearly</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">00</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> restaurants as of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">September</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> &nbsp;3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle is ranked on the Fortune 500 and is recognized on the 2022 list for Fortune&#x2019;s Most Admired Companies. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">With </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">100</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,000 em</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">ployees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the fo</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">od industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. For more information or to place an order online, visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 3pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">RECONCILIATION OF NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk22568764"></a><font style="display: inline;">The following tables provide a reconciliation of non-GAAP financial measures presented in the text above to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adjusted net income is net income excluding expenses related to </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">restaurant asset impairment, corporate restructuring, legal proceedings, stock-</font><font style="display: inline;">based compensation modification expense, unrealized gains on equity investments, </font><font style="display: inline;">separation costs, </font><font style="display: inline;">and certain other costs. Adjusted general and administrative expense is general and administrative expense excluding transformation expenses, legal proceedings, stock-based compensation modification expense, </font><font style="display: inline;">separation costs, </font><font style="display: inline;">and certain other costs. The adjusted effective income tax rate is the effective income tax rate adjusted to reflect the after tax impact of non-GAAP adjustments. Restaurant Level Operating Margin, a non-GAAP financial measure, is equal to the revenues generated by our restaurants less their direct operating costs which consist of food, beverage and packaging, labor, occupancy and other operating costs. This performance measure primarily includes the costs that restaurant level managers can directly control and excludes other costs that are essential to conduct our business. Management uses restaurant level operating margin as a measure of restaurant performance. Management believes restaurant level operating margin is useful to investors in that it highlights trends in our core business that may not otherwise be apparent to investors when relying solely on GAAP financial measures. We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, adjusted general and administrative expenses, adjusted effective income tax rate and restaurant level operating margin measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
		</p>
